Here is what you need to know:\n\nWhen: The draft will be held over three days, from Thursday, April 25 through Saturday, April 27. The first round will be held Thursday starting at 8 p.m., the second and third rounds begin Friday at 7 p.m. and the final four rounds will be held Saturday starting at noon. All times are Eastern.\n\nWhere: Detroit.\n\nTelevision/radio: ESPN will air coverage on Thursday and Saturday, ESPN and ESPN2 will split Friday, and ABC, NFL Network and ESPN Deportes will offer coverage all three days. The ESPN app will cover all three days for streamers. Those that can't watch can listen on ESPN Radio.\n\nWho holds the No. 1 pick? The Chicago Bears. The first round will be held Thursday starting at 8 p.m., the second and third rounds begin Friday at 7 p.m. and the final four rounds will be held Saturday starting at noon.
